 1
 agar offis main kisi ko pasand kar baithe hai or us kii taraf se koi pratikriya nahin ai he, to ghabaraaen nahin
 Whenever he is in a meeting, busy elsewhere, help him in his work
 phir dekhie kaise vah dhire-dhire aapako apana hero bana leti he
 2
 agar aap kii garlfriend ko pats pasand hai, to us ke saath hi saath us pats ko bhi apana mureed bana len
 This does not mean that you will have to take your girlfriend's dog or make it a morning walk
 jab kabhi us ke ghar jaaen, to kutton ke liye kuch biscuit le jaaen
 That's enough for them to like you
 3
 Keep mailing them from time to time
 yah jaruri nahin ki aap koi kaam hone par yaa phir kisi utsav par hi unhen mail yaa messej karen
 Get into the habit of sending one email daily and one morning message
 is se vah dur hote hue bhi aap ko vah philings de sakati hai ki aap romanchit hue bina nahin rah paaenge
 4
 aphis ke kaam main madad karne ke saath hi saath apni garlfriend ke liye kabhi kabhi kuch-kuch karenge, to vah aap ko khub pyaar degi
 Do not think that you do not know how to cook or what you will make for her, which will make her happy
 bas jo bhi aasaan lage, bana lijie, chahen to megi yaa popcorn hi bana len
 Surely this path will reach their heart directly
 5
 Read the newspaper daily or watch the news so that you are aware of the surrounding topics
 local akhbaar kii bajaae rashtriya yaa videshi khabaron par najar rakhen
 The advantage of this is that whenever there are situations of unwanted or unintentional debates in front of you, you can still impress your partner or girlfriend without losing your confidence
 6
 Do not just say words like sorry

 is prakaar landan olympic main bharat kaa naukayan pratiyogita main chunauti ab samaapt ho gai he

 is prakaar sina ko bhagya ke sahare kaansya padak praapt ho gaya
 World's fifth seed Saina is the second woman from India to win a medal in the Olympic individual event
 landan olympic main bharat kaa yah teesraa padak he
 Earlier, shooter Gagan Narang has won bronze and Vijay Kumar has given silver to India
 vishwa kii purv sheersh or vartmaan kii nambar do khilaadi wang kaa ghutana smash lagane ke liye uchhalane par chotil ho gaya

 padak ke prabal daavedaaron main se ek mukkebaaz lashram devendro singh (49 kilogram) ne quarter final main jagah bana liya he
 Devendro defeated Mongolia's Cerdamba Purevdorj 16-11 in the pre-quarterfinal match
 devendra ne shuruyaat se hi aakraamak rukh akhriyaar kiya or use match ke ant tak jari rakhaa

 of Honduras
 boron se tha

 mahila nishanebaaj shagun choudhary trep spardhaa ke final main sthaan banane se chook gayi
 Shagun finished 20th in qualifying
 shagun ne pehle round main 20 kaa score kiya lekin agle do round main vah kramash: 17 or 21 kaa score kar sakin
 He scored a total of 61
 italy kii jesica rosi kwalifing main sheersh par rahete hue final main jagah banaain

 bharat ke navik sandip kumaar or manajit singh purush linewet yugal scals spardhaa ke final main antim sthaan par aane se batch gaye or vah 19wein sthaan par rahe
 Sandeep and Manjeet took seven minutes 8 in this event held at Eton Dorney Lake
 39 second samay ke saath 19wein sthaan par rahe
 Sandeep and Manjeet remained one notch above the last

 eksrasij ko physical fitness ke liye behad jaruri samajha jaataa he

 badhati umr ke saath vyakti kaa dimag kamjor padane lagata he

 darasal, eksrasij karne se dimag par bahut acha asar padataa he

 ye hai eksrasij karne ke phaayde-1
 Make the memory sharp - It has been confirmed in many studies that regular exercise increases memory
 yaaddaasht ko tej karne main cardio yaa aerobics eksrasij sabase ahm hai
 2
 smart banaae-- ek research ke mutabik, eksrasij karne se brain dirivd neurotrophic factor (BDNF) protein dimag main nikalataa he
 This protein works to make new cells of the brain and helps in remembering things quickly
 3
 Relieve stress - Exercising daily helps a person to be safe from stress
 isliye jab bhi aapako tanaav mahasoos ho to eksrasij jarur karen
 4
 mood behatar kare-- kisi bhi prakaar kii eksrasij karne se mood acha hota he

 On Thursday, Haryana Chief Minister Manohar Lal Khattar announced a grant of one million rupees to the family of former soldier Ramkishan Grewal and a job to a member but said it was not right to call Ramkishan a martyr
 ek tarah se khatter sahab kii baat thik bhi he lekin unki duusari baat se ardhsainik bal ke jawan ko raahat mil sakati he
 Khattar Saheb said that the one who dies on the border is the martyr, so why are the soldiers of the paramilitary forces not considered martyrs
 purv sainik ramkishan greval kaa antim sanskaar unke gaanv main kiya gaya

 subah subah ramkishan greval ke gaanv pahunche the

 uskaa maamla bank kaa tha

 use kisne sulphas kii tablet di

 His village is a short distance from the village of Ramkishan Grewal
 bhaajapa netaa siddharth nath singh ne kaha ki rahul gandhi ne van rank van pension ko lekar kabhi kuch nahin kiya
 We have also formed a committee to correct its shortcomings
 bijepi ke saansad satyapal singh ne kaha ki unhen lagata he ki dilli police ne is masale ko thik se handle nahin kiya he
 There is no problem in meeting the family of an ex-soldier
 shahanwaaz hossain ne kaha ki sena ke itane jawan shahid hue, unke antim sanskaar main to congress netaa or rahul gandhi nahin gaye
 If someone has committed suicide, they are doing politics
 shahanwaaz kaa nishaanaa thodaa sahi jagah laga he
 The comments bhaajapa netaa nalin kohli ne kaha ki ghatana dukhad he magar ye congress ke liye photo oparchunity ban gaya he
 But even after this criticism of Congress BJP, it has started looking active in this matter
 aam aadmi party bhi kaaphi sakriy he

 lekin rahul gandhi ko police ne apni girftar main le liya
 Rahul Gandhi has been detained for the third time in two days
 rahul gandhi ko sansad maarg thane main le jaaya gaya, baad main tughlaq road thane le jaae gaye

 congress kahati he ijazat lee gai thi

 Do the work of these people
 hamako to koi or bhi kaam mil jayega
 
 kar lenge'
 In the new government, the matter of yoga went ahead
 
 When PM Modi himself joined it, one and a half lakh people with a Bachelor of Physical Education degree would be hoping that the demand for their jobs would increase, but only 32,000 people who were tested here got their job lost
 bipied sangharsh morcha ke adhyaksh dhirendra pratap yadav kaa kahana he ki 'ek taraf to mananeey yogi ji or mananeey pradhanmantri ji yoga ko badhaava dene ke liye 21 june ko yoga diwas manaate hai
 
 jameen par aakar khud baithte hai
 
 janata ko ye dikhaane kaa prayaas karte hai ki ham yoga ko badhaava dete hai, lekin jab tak shaareerik shikshakon kii niyukti nahin hogi, jo garib pariwaron ke bachche skool main pard rahe hai, unako yoga kaise sikhaaya ja saktaa he'
 The comments nai sarkaar kaa iljaam he ki akhilesh sarkaar ke dauraan bhartiyon main bahut bade paimaane par gadbadiyaan hui hai
 All the recruitments were banned by the courts
 upi public sarvice kamishan ke chairman ko bhi bhartiyon main ghotaale ke iljaam main adaalat ne hataaya
 In such a situation, transparency and honesty is being investigated in these recruitments
 bhaajapa ke media incharge harishchandra shrivastav ne kaha ki, 'jis tarah kaa bhrashtachar samaajawaadee party kii sarkaar main niyuktiyon ko lekar tha, vah aam tha
 Eligible children were getting frustrated
 yogi ji kii sarkaar kaa agenda bilkul saaf he ki ham ek paardarshee vyavastha den
 In that transparent arrangement so that fair appointments can be made
 jo yogya abhyarthi hai, unako sthaan mil sake'
 Dheerendra Pratap Yadav, Chairman of BPED Sangharsh Morcha, says that '32,000 posts have been created for us till the mandate has been issued
 ham logon ne form bhar diya or jaise hi satta parivartan hua, mananeey yogi ji kii sarkaar bani or tab se is bhartee prakiya par roak laga di gai'
 Tents along the river have fallen due to rain water
 tamaam tambu ukhd gaye hai
 
 kuch apane bhiige tents sukhaane kii jugat main hai, to kuch ne paas ke fliover ke neeche panaah lee he
 In the previous regime too, they used to get lathis on seeking jobs
 is sarkaar main bhi laathiyaan padi hai
 The Subordinate Services Selection Commission laid off around 11,500 jobs
 kareeb 4,000 log likhit pariksha main paas hue, kuch kaa intervyuu bhi hua, lekin bhartee par roak lag gai
 Suraj Pandey, a candidate for the post of Junior Assistant, says that the future of all our students is steeped in balance
 samaj main nahin aa rahaa ki sarkaar hamen job dena chaahati he yaa nahin dena chaahati
 We are still relying on the assurance that the government will provide us a good job, but the deadline continues to drag on for a long time
 kya ham berozegaron kii jindagi aisi hi khinchati hui chali jaaegi'
 At the same time, Amit Yadav, a candidate for the post of Junior Assistant, said that 'everyone in our family is sitting with hope
 sabhi ke gharon main log aas laga ke baithe hai
 We are unemployed students
 agar hamamen se koi ek aage nahin aayega to ham apni maangon ko sarkaar tak kaise pahunchaayenge'
 These students live in their camps located in the sunny shore
 yahaan se inaki awaz hukumat tak media ke jariye hi pahunchati he
 BTC and TET trained people are also struggling for jobs here
 yah kehete hai ki basic shiksha mantri ne inase kaha ki naukari nahin mil sakati, kyonki 65,000 shikshak zyada hai
 They found out from the RTI that there is a shortage of 1
5 lakh teachers
 shikshak pad ke ummidavaar vikaas verma ne kaha ki 'ham log 75,000 bhartiyon kii maang kar rahe hai, lekin 90 din se zyada ho gaye hai, lekin sarkaar kii taraf se abhi tak na koi aashwaasan mila he, na hi inhone apana koi vaada puraa kiya he'
 Siraj manages his livelihood in this crowd of job seekers
 yahaan thele par pani bechate hai
 Some cold drinks also sell, etc
 inke saath rahete-rahete inhen bhi sabaki takaliphen pataa chal gai hai
 They themselves pray for their jobs
 siraaj kehete hai, 'in logon ke saath insaaf hona chahie
 For so many days, the hungry and thirsty are lying in the rain
 lekin agar in logon ko nyaay mil jayega or ye yahaan se chale jaaenge to aapkaa kaam kaise chalegaa, is sawaal ke jawaab main siraaj kaa kahana he ki 'yahaan par bahut saare log apana dukh-dard lekar aate rahete hai
 We also suffer because poor people leave their homes and come here
 itane-itane din pade rahete hai

 Do the work of these people
 hamako to koi or bhi kaam mil jayega
 
 kar lenge'

 dpendra Pratap Yadav, Chairman of BPED Sangharsh Morcha, said that 'on the one hand, Honorable Yogi Ji and Hon'ble Prime Minister celebrate Yoga Day on 21 June to promote Yoga
 
 Coming to the ground and sitting on their own
 
 We try to show the public that we promote yoga, but until the appointment of physical teachers, children of poor families studying in school, how can they be taught yoga '
 tippaniyan The new government alleges that during the Akhilesh government, there have been a large number of disturbances in the recruitment
 tamaam bhartiyon par adaalaton ne roak lagaai thi
 The chairman of the UP Public Service Commission was also removed by the court in the charges of recruitment
 aise main in bhartiyon main paardarshita or eemaandaaree kii jaanch kii ja rahi he
 bjp's media in-charge Harishchandra Shrivastava said, 'the kind of corruption that was involved in appointments in the Samajwadi Party government was common
 yogya bachche kunthit ho rahe the
 The agenda of Yogi ji's government is very clear that we should provide a transparent system
 us paardarshee vyavastha main taaki nishpaksh niyuktiyaan ho saken
 Those who are qualified candidates can get a place '

 7 of these day shifters

 One needs to be careful if you also use toilet paper
 toilet paper kaa istemaal karne se aapako swasthya sambandhi kai bimaariyaan ho sakati hai
 In countries such as Japan, Italy and Greece, people use toilet water (bide) while countries like Britain, America and Australia use toilet paper
 lekin ab doctors iske gambhir parinaamon ke prati aagaah kar rahe hai
 According to experts, using toilet paper does not make you completely clean
 toilet paper ke zyada istemaal se urinary tract infections (UTI) or enal fisher jaisi bimaariyaan hone kaa khatra bad jaataa he
 Expert Ros George says, it bothers me that people are moving around with dirt when they think they are absolutely clean
 toilet paper se poti idhar-udhar fail jaati he jabaki yah puri tarah se gandagi saaf nahin karata he
 Even if you find it strange, George is not alone
 kai celibrity tak keval toilet paper kii jagah wet wips kaa istemaal kar rahe hai
 Let us understand this with an example
 kuch chocolate lijie or ise farsh par failaa dijie or phir ise sookhe towel se saaf karne kii koshish kariye
 Chocolate will be seen in pieces
 keval safai hi nahin balki toilet paper ke anya vikalpon par sochane kii or bhi vajahen hai

 is beemaari se ubarne main afko 8 se 12 hafte lag jate hai

 isse infections hone kii sambhaavna bhi kam ho jaati he

 The weather system built in the Bay of Bengal has turned into a deep depression, but it is becoming more powerful in its place
 mausam vibhaag ke mutabik agle kuch ghanton main ye wedar system ek chakravaati tufaan kaa vikaraal rup dhaaran kar legaa
 So far, the deep depression is about 550 km north-east direction from Port Blair
 is samay is wedar system ke andar 55 se 65 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar se hawaaen umad-ghumad rahi hai
 Based on the information received from the weather radar and satellite, it is estimated that this weather system will turn into a cyclone on the morning of 25th
 jab ye wedar system cyclone yanichakravaati tufanmen tabdeel hoga, to ye samandar ke andar hi hoga or iske andar chal rahi hawaaon kii raftaar 70 se 80 kilometre prati ghante kii raftaar par pahunch jaaegi
 According to the Cyclone Center, after the formation of Cyclone, it will be named Cyclone and it is the name given to Myanmar
 mausam vibhaag ke ediji em mahapaatr ke mutabik is baar jo cyclone banane ja rahaa he wo ek durlabh kism kii ghatana he

 15 july, 1958 ko bihar ke mujffarpur paidaa hui suman kesari ne jawaharlal nehru vishvavidhyalay se surdaas par shogh kiya he tathaa uniwarsity of western australia perth se emb kiya
 She has been associated with administration related to Government of India and later academic work
 unhone 'jeenyu main namvar singh' naamak pustak kaa sampadan kiya
 With his poetic collection titled 'arguments from Yajnavalkya', 'monalisa's eyes', 'words and dreams' and 'in the folds of pyramids', he has made a considerable identity in the literary world
 raajakmal prakaashan se prakashit 'pyramidon kii tahon main' naamak kavy-sangrah ke parichay main ashok kumaar pandeya ne likhaa he ki suman keshari kaa kavy sansar vistrut behad he
 This expansion is also horizontal and vertical
 ve gam-e-dauraan tak bhi jaati hai or gam-e-janaa tak bhi
 She wanders from myths to dreams to identify the sorrows of the material world, and also to struggle daily for the expansion of the volume of the soul
 "lagbhag teen dashakon ke apane sakriy jivan main suman kesari ne lagaataar apane samay or samaaj kii hulchalon ko unki jatil bidambanaaon ke saath darj karne kaa prayaas to kiya hi he, saath hi ek stri ke liye, jo saajha or alag abhidharth ho sakate hai, unhen bahut spasht taur par abhilakshith bhi kiya hai
 "in the roaring darkness of the pyramid's folds, 'where there is not a single drop of water, there is a heat', in this attempt to collect life's life for humanity by searching through the lines of light, their relationship with tradition is dialectical
 ek ore gaharaa anuraag to duusari ore ek satat asantosh
 The most condensed form of Suman Keshari's concerns are seen in a poem like 'words and Dreams'
 chote-chote nau khandon main banti yah lambi kavita apane puure vitan main pathak ke man main bhay hi nahin paidaa karti balki samakaleen vartmaan kaa ek aisa drishy nirmit karti hai, jahow iske shilp main antarvinyast bechaini pathak kii aatma tak utarkar mukti kii chaah or uske liye manushyata ke aakhri bache chinhon ko bachaa lene kaa adamya sankalp bhi bharti he
 "suman is an integral part of Kesari's poetic world
" ‘maan kii aankhon ke jal main tirane' kii kaamana ke saath, apane jivan main mukti or sangharsh karti swapnon se yatharth ke bich nirantar awajahi karti ‘kirnon kaa sira tham lene’ kaa swapn dekhati vah yah bhi jaanati he ki 'chonch ke sparsh bina ghar nahin banataa’ or yah bhi ki 'aurat hi ghar banaati he / par jab bhi baat hoti he ghar kii / to vah hameshaa mard kaa hi hota he
 "" In this women's sensory world, along with humans, there is also nature, so motherless children and unborn children too
 jivan ke har safe par likhe 'asambhav' se takaraati or ‘ghar kii tarah ghar main rahane' hi nahin ‘sangeenon ke saae tale prem karne kii adamya jijivishaa se bhari suman keshari kii ye kavitaayen samakaleen kavita ke ruksh vaataavaran main myth, lok or swapn kaa ek bhavy vaatayan hi srujit nahin karatin apitu prem, karuna or audaarya ke maanviya jivmulyon par aadhaarit ek samanvayvaadee vitan bhi rachati hai jisamen bhavishya ke swapn dekhe ja saken
 Read on Suman Kesari's birthday on Sahitya Aaj Tak, selected poems from his poetic collection called 'in the folds of pyramids': 1
 ye din pyramidon kii tahon main guzarate din hanye din pyramidon kii tahon main guzarate din hanghupp andheron main basii he
 The stench of poison has become a poisonous stone, the snake crawls beneath the mud, the bones are awakening, only the horrors are awakening from the realization of life
 The third journey was
 teen baar pukaarane par pret jaagate hai
 It was said that Guru i called the Guru three times three souls started to follow me
 Guru was echoing in Kopiramid
